event {
    internal {
        fix-confd-rollback {
            type    directory-watch;
            path    /opt/versa/confd/var/confd/rollback;
            scripts [ fixrollback.sh ];
        }
        on-cpu-or-mem-high-alarm {
            type    ipc;
            id      vmod-cpu-or-mem-high;
            scripts [ vmod_top_dump.sh ];
        }
        on-debug-fileadd {
            type    directory-watch;
            path    /var/tmp/versa-debug;
            scripts [ run_debug_cmds.sh ];
        }
        on-device-reset-keypress {
            type    ipc;
            id      device-reset;
            scripts [ device_reset.lua ];
        }
        on-key-fileadd {
            type    directory-watch;
            path    /home/versa/keys;
            scripts [ accept_key.lua ];
        }
        on-nc-connect-long-time {
            type    ipc;
            id      vmod-clear-restrns;
            scripts [ clear-restrn.sh ];
        }
        on-trial-filerm {
            type    directory-watch;
            path    /var/lib/vs;
            scripts [ trial_chk.lua ];
        }
        usb-storage-for-staging {
            type    directory-watch;
            path    /var/run/versa/usb;
            scripts [ do_usb_stage.sh ];
        }
        vsmd-health-check-debug {
            type    ipc;
            id      vsmd-health-check-debug;
            scripts [ /opt/versa/scripts/health_check_debug.sh ];
        }
        vsmd-mgmt-connection-down {
            type    ipc;
            id      vsmd-mgmt-connection-down;
            scripts [ dorollback.sh ];
        }
        when-key-about-to-expire {
            type    operational;
            id      vstrial-alert;
            scripts [ key_abt2expire.lua ];
        }
    }
